25b3(rgyud): mtshan nyid do// rtsangs pa'i 'dod chags mnyam gnas so// zur sel phra dog lhas spyod no// nor rgyal gti mug bdag nyid de/ srog gi rlung ni grangs gnyis las// dga'i ba'i can zhes bya/ skyo ba de yas btags pa'o// 
25b4(rgyud): de phyir mkhas pas so sor shes pa'i sa// gang phyir srog gi rlung ni bad+ma gnyid skyo// ji ltar sa'i bcu gnyis las la// thog ma de nyid bcu gnyis pa'o// bcu po rnams kyis de shes bya/ gang phyiri sa bcu'i
25b5(rgyud): dbang phyug go// sa gcig rang bzhin rnams kyis ni/ rdo rje 'dzin mchen mor 'dod// sbyin bsregs pha rol phyin pa gang / lhan skye yang dag byang chub nyid/ thams cad kyi ni nang son pas// rdo rje
25b6(rgyud): dbyings dbang phyug ma mchog ma/ gshang dang ma gshang gang ci'ang rung / de kun byang chub tshul can no// slar yang bya rog dbyabs lha mo// de na byed pa'i gnas can mo// byed pa'i gos kyi gnas la ste/ rtswa rnams
25b7(rgyud): kun gi bug ste/ tha mi dang de las langs bsam gtan// kha gdong ma tu 'du shes so// de ltar rnal 'byor thams cad/ bla ma'i zhal las gsal thob 'gyur/ bla ma gang de mi nus shing / bston byas de bzhin
25b8(rgyud): 'dod par bya/ 'phags pa'i go 'phang ma thob pa/ mnar med la sogs rnam su 'byed/ kun nas bla ma gus pa las/ byang chub bar du thob par 'gyur/ dpa' bo tha~Md mnyam sbyor las rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mtsho
26a1(rgyud): rdo rje 'kha 'gro de gshegs/ bcom ldan bdag pos 'di gsungs so// zhes bya ba ni dpal 'kha'agro rgya mtsho rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po las/ kha gdong ma la sogs pa'i srog bskyed pa'i
26a2(rgyud): mtsham nyid kyi cho ga ste// le'u bdun pa'o// de nas gzhan gyi mtshan nyid mchog/ 'ug gdong la sogs gang gsal ba// byed pa yang dag byed pa dang / thams cad mtshams ni bshad par bya// 'khrig
26a3(rgyud): pa yi ni snod rnams kyi/ zla ba'i gzugs kyis rtag tu gnas/ 'ug gdong ye shes thob nas ni/ rtsa ni lan gsum 'gro ba mo/ drag shul gzi rjid rtsigs pa mo// yis la dbang za ba las/ le'u 'dod la
26a4(rgyud): dga' ba 'phrul che// lA mni la sogs skye rnams la// rkang pa'i 'theb mthar bcu gnyis la/ ka mda'i shugs kyis 'gro bar 'gyur// shug gdong ma'i mang las yang // u ni ur+yan bu gar 'dod// 
26a5(rgyud): la pu l+li ra ma la yang grags// u ni mu ma mu ni zhing ngo // ka ni kA ma ru ba ste/ de bzhin su 'dir zhing kun 'dod/ zhang kun dbus su gyur pa ni/ gru gsum pa'i bde ba'i mtha'/ gang phyir gnas
26a6(rgyud): lnga'i bdag nyid kyi/ mi zad he ru ka'i gro 'phang ngo // yang na bdag gi bdan gsogs su/ dpal he ru ka rdo rje rang / skye gnas rnam kyi bdag nyid de/ snying lte dkan dang 'go bo dang / gsang ba ru yang rtsa kun gyi
26a7(rgyud): skye gnas bu ga lnga bdag nyid/ sgong skyes dang ni brod sher skyes/ mngal skyes rdzus te skye ba rnams/ sems sangs rgyas yon tan bdag/ rigs lnga rab tu bsngon pa'o// nye ba'i gling du gnas pa yang / gtso bo'i
26a8(rgyud): gzugs can yang dag gnas// sngags kyi 'phreng ba las skyes rnams/ sum bcu rtsa gsum bdag nyid skyes/ oM ba mdza hA u ka lU lA ka ka s+ya ga ni ya sam ke ni hU~M b+ha hU~M ya pa hU~M Ta hU~M pha phaT Ta sA pha ha na oM
26b1(rgyud): swa hUM ha/ de ltar sngags de na'i bdag/ shes rab thabs kyi bdag nyid can// kha gdong ljang ser brag chen mo// lhag ma la ma dang ni mtshungs// dkyil 'khor dbus su bsgom byas nas// dud khrod gnas dang gnyis me
26b2(rgyud): pa// kun spyod rtsa rnams thaMd kyi/ rgyas pa'i dga' ba'i spyod yul lo// 'di ni mtsho ba'i ting 'dzin dang / 'od gsal rnam pa'i chos nyid do// smad pa'i las dang rnal 'byor ma// 'jig rten gyi ni 'dren pa mo// rang gi bstan
26b3(rgyud): chos la ga gsungs pa'i// sna tshogs las kyang bya ba'o// kun gyi rnal 'byor yongasu rdzogs nas/ rgyud 'di yi ni spyod yul lo// 'on kyang rnal 'byor de kun kyang / mdor bsdus tshul ni nyid ya ni/ so sor bsdud dang
26b4(rgyud): de bzhin du/ bsam gtan srog rtsol 'dzin pa dang // rjes su bran dang tang 'dzin te// sbyor ba'i mtshan nyid rnam drug go// so sor skud pa Sha rdong ma'o// 'ug rjong ma ni bsam gtan 'dod // srog rtse la du ni gan
26b5(rgyud): pa khyi/ 'dzin pa la ni phag ma'o// rjes bran gnas pa pho nya'o// ting nge 'dzin ni rten mar 'dod// 'che ba ma ni rgyas bstan thob// 'dzes ma 'bras bu kun bdag skyes/ 'khor ba las ni grol gyur pa/ 
26b6(rgyud): rang gi sku ni sgyu ma mnyam// bdag sbyin rlabs 'di ni phra mo dang / rdo rje zlas rang mtshan nyid do// rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi gter// de las lhag ma bzung ba 'jug// mya ngan 'das zhes bya ba 'dri/ lam thams cad kyis
26b7(rgyud): mya ngan 'das// theg chen kun la rab 'jug pa// sngags kyi theg pa ru ni byed// bya ba sman chos dge sna tshogs// snying rje rnyes shan pa yas byed// gang 'bru'i dngos dang dngos po la// ye shes rnam par rang 'byung gis// 
26b8(rgyud): de 'dra ba yi sems rgyun las/ bdag nyid rnal 'byor rnams kyis mthong // lus kyi mtshan nyid yang dag pa// rtsa'i gur ni bshad par bya// spyi rtsug nas ni nor bu'i mthar// 'chos dang 'bran pa rnam gnyis 'dod// rkang / 
27a1(rgyud): pa'i 'the bong ma chos mtha' dang / sAni dus de bzhin slob ste/ mtshan ma'i rtsirtsa 'bral bdag/ mig dang gang pa'i sor mo gnyis/ mang med dang ni pus mo gnyis/ rgyas brna pa gnyis dag dang / rkang ngan
27a2(rgyud): 'brel dang snying dag dang // lte ba dang ni rgya bzhung dang // gshang le dang ni rkan shes bya// rkang pa'i tshigs dang mchu dag dang / 'khur ba 'khur tshos dang ni// 'doms dang mchan khung gnyis dang ni// lag pa'i tshigs dang rkang pa dag/ dpung pa'i tshigs
27a3(rgyud): dang nu ma gnyis// 'dzad pa thal gong 'dir mtsham so// 'jug ma nor bu gnyis dag dang // kyed pa'i tshig dang 'grin pa dang / bral ba dang ni tshags gnyis dag/ rna bug dag dang rtsa ba dang / brang dag gnyis kyi 'tsham su 'dod// bstan dag gnyi
27a4(rgyud): dang smin khung dang / lte dang mi'i sna gong dang / de bzhin tu ni rkan dang lce// bo la ka k+ko la gnyis dag/ de la sogs pa tu ma ni/ rtsa dang chags kyi gnad du 'gyur// rang rang mchod pa tsari byas te// byang sems bdag nyid che rnams kyi// tsan
27a5(rgyud): thabs sbyor ba'i cho ga ru/ shes bya bla ma'i gsung gis so// zla bzla yAM chos gang dang / chos grangs de la rtsa ba'i rtsi/ dkar po tshes gcig laso gas nas// ji sri nag po'i thar thug pa/ shes rab byang chub 'bab pa'i rtsa/ 
27a6(rgyud): 'ug mo skal spyod pa mo// gang dang 'dra ba'i gdong de yi/ de 'dra'i sor me'i phyag l+ya ni// dbugs ni de dang 'dra bar bya/ phyi ding nang gi bdag nyid 'dod/ yang na rtsa rnams thams cad ni/ btsir bya bcu gnyis kyis lhag pa'i// rgya'i tshigs rnaMs tha
27a7(rgyud): ni/ dza ltar gdong bi rim pas so// de dang dar ni a li 'bar// dran po'i sgyu ma dus kun tu// de phya ri a zhes bya ba'i sgo// tshig tu rtogs pas rtags pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbugs dbyung bar/ rdo rje 'chang ltar rtag pa'o// 
27a8(rgyud): gang dang gisi 'ching 'gyur ba/ rtsa ni gti mug chen por 'gyur/ de las de'i rang bzhin 'gyur/ sna tshogs gzugs ni rang bzhin 'gyur/ tshangs dang 'khas rnams kyi dag la/ mnga' bdag thar pa chen po zhugs/ byed pa poni
27b1(rgyud): thaMd kyi// dbang phyug skye bo sna tshogs rnams// de phyir rtag tu la nyams pa// sngon byas sdig pa'i las byis te// nyes gyur bstan pa 'di las ni/ dgod bya sangs rgyas nyid thob 'gyur/ dpa'o thams cad mnyam sbyor las// rdo rje
27b2(rgyud): sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje 'kha 'gro de bzhin gshegs/ bcom ldan bdag pos 'di gsungaso// zhes bya ba ni dpal 'kha' gro rgya mtsho rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po las// 'ug gdong ma'i de'i ba'i tshul dang // yang
27b3(rgyud): dag pa'i cho ga las skyed pa dang / srog la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid kyi le'u ste/ rgyad pa'o// de nas gzhan gyi don chen po// khyi gdong rgyu'i dbye bshad bya/ gang zhig rnam par shes tsam gyis/ rnal 'byor rnams kyi chog
27b4(rgyud): 'gyur// sA khyi ni rnal 'byor ma dbugs 'byin 'gyur// rang gis 'a jug dang 'byung bar 'gyur// dus kun tu ni gnyid log dang // sad pa bde ba yon tan che// sna tshogs gnas su song nas ni// bdag nyid kyi ni
27b5(rgyud): de rig 'gyur/ rgyal nyi shus lhag par ni// des tshig bstan mtshan nyid do// de ltar gyi'i mni tu naM/ bde ba byin pa por zhes bya/ dad ma'i skye gnas de rnas su// a s+yA pad ma'i Sha ni rang rgyas pa
27b6(rgyud): gdong dang 'ong spyod gar chen po// klu dang rol mo gnyid log dang / reg dang gos dang rgyan dag dang / me tog la sogs gsung can 'dod// mthun par lta ba'i ma la sogs// 'dzes ma rnams kyi ngag can te/ sangs rgyas mchod sngogs
27b7(rgyud): zad du/ su ra'i btud las 'thung 'gyur dang / bskyed mos tshal dang rdzang bu'i 'bram// sti gnas 'gro ba la sogs kyis/ tshami dang bston mo 'dod pa ltar/ bla ma'i gsung na bde chen po// mi dang mi mo'i skyeg pa dang // rgod pa skyeg pa'i bya/ 
27b8(rgyud): ba gang // mkhas pa rnaMs kyi 'di dam pa// skye bo dbang phyug nyid du'o// sangs rgyas chos dang dge 'dun la/ mchod bya mchod byed la sogs pas// bla ma la gus bde ba sngar// yon dbul ba dang bud med do// spyod rnams la sogs chos
27b9(rgyud): rnams la/ las thams lngas mi 'jug go// dkrol ba rnaMs kyis gzhom pa dang / sangs rgyas chos la bzhag pa dang // rnal 'byor ma dang bza' btung dang / skam dang dga' ba skyed pa dang / dbang po gnyis kyi dga' ba dang / sbyin
28a1(rgyud): sogs pa rol phyin rnams kyi/ las kyi skyi btsal bya dang / byas dang snying rje dga' ba dang / kun gyi tha mar btang snyoms dang / ye shes rnam shes smra ba dang / dbu ma'i tshul las bzhag pa las/ kun la dbugs dbyu
28a2(rgyud): sbyin pa dang / skur ba 'debs pa dgag pa dang / dge ba bcu'i las dang ni/ glog dang kha dog byed mchog dang // byang chub lam la gnas pa yi/ dpa' bo gnyis med lta ba'i phyir/ lus la ltos med pa yis// grong dang grong du gnas rnams
28a3(rgyud): kyi// de ltar gnas bskabs gcig pa'o// gnyis pa slar yang bshad pa'o// sangs rgyas rnams kyi rgyud la dga'/ don dam rnams la gsal ba yis// rnal 'byor ma rnams kyi gnas su// dngos grub rnam gnyis brjod pa dang /

61a3(rgyud): ye brta tsa kra ya hU~M d+ha ma te we hUM mu kha ya hUM ne shan tra ya hU~M ka ba la ma ni hU~M b+hu dza ya hU~M A sta a ya hU~M tsa ra na ya hUM/ dza ra na na ya hU~M dza Ta ma khu Ta// ya ma sa ga sag sa ra sa ra b+ha ra b+ha ra ma ra ma ra tra Ta tra Ta g+ha tra g+ha Ta ma
61a4(rgyud): mu nya tsa g+ho ra ra nad+da ka ra pri ya ya phi phi phud phud ra ma ra ma ba ra mAtha ru pe ni shan ti ka re ye puSh+Ta bar+t+ta nI yo lo ka pa la ru bi ne sarba sha ri ra ru pa ye bri kra gu lu la tA ya sa sma ru be Ne sarba ba stu ne ma ra Na ya
61a5(rgyud): ma ra pa Na ru pa ya b+ha kra ya na ru pa ya ri ro ba ma ya ni ba ma su kha be he sa bi la sa bi las/ nri t+ta ni t+ye pa ya ni t+ya yA ba ya di dri ya yo g+ho ya ni sarba wa ma ha da ma ne sha sta d+ha ra ni wa ra ni ya nA nA tsa ra tsa ra/ 
61a6(rgyud): tsha de ni tsu pa tsu ba hU~M lu hu lu tsu lu tsu lu/ hU~M hU~M ha hU~M ha hU~M ha~M hU~M hU hU~M hu hU~M he hU~M he hUM ho hU~M ho hU~M/ he hU~M he hU~M/ hU~M hU~M hriM hriM dzu dzu kr-i kri pheM pa~M phu dzu/ yoM pheM pheM pa~M pa~M pha/ ku tsa ku tsa tra Ta tra Ta/ ma Ta ma Ta ra dza ra tha ra/ da dza da tha/ dzaHdza
61a7(rgyud): thA/ ma da ma da/ hUM hU~M hUM hUM hUM hUMHhU~M hUM hUM hUM hUM/ phaT swA hA// // rtsa ba'i sngags// dpa' bo thams cad mnyam sbyor bas// rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje 'kha' 'gro de bzhin gshegs// bzhin bcom/ 
61a8(rgyud): ldan bdag pos 'di gsungs so// zhes bya ba ni 'kha' 'gro rgya mtsho rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po las/ rtsa ba'i sngags btu ba'i cho ga'i mtshan nyid kyi le'u ste bcu drug pa'o// de nas gzhan
61b1(rgyud): yang bshad bya ba/ lus can rnams kyis go cha ste// rdo rje sems dpa' snying kha ru/ a li dang sbyor rgyas bdab bya/ rdo rje snying po'i ye shes dang / sems dpa' na mkha' dang gcig pa// snying kha rnam pa khra mo/ 
61b2(rgyud): ste/ a li gtum mo yum yin no// lus can sbyor ba'ang mi 'gyur zhes bya ba/ 'di ltar dbang po kun rgyas bdab// phyir srung ba'ang oM ha yi ga/ yig gang rtag tu 'joms med pa'o// lhag ma rnam snang rjod/ 
61b3(rgyud): pa'i mthar// rdo rje skyod pa las sgra'o// de'i phyir ji ltar mngon par ni/ rjod pa las ni bzhengs pa'i gzugs/ mi rnams kyi ni snying dbus su// sum bcu bdun bdag nyid dkyil 'khor// rdo rje sems dpa' mo
61b4(rgyud): 'khyud pa'ang / lte ba'i 'khor lor bsrung ba ste/ oM baM gi ni snga gas kyi gzugs// dbu ma 'dzes dang rdo rje dang // kha sbyor 'di ni bsrung ba che// ma byung dad par yang dag byung // 'khor lo kun gyi bsang
61b5(rgyud): sngags kyis// dngos grub kun gsal bshang byar bya// oM haHta baM hi ba~M hi bi thu bu hu pu he be he pre// he be he bo ha be ha ga/ hUMhU~M hU~M phaT phaT phaT srad+d+ha/ zung dang ring po'i rang bzhin gis// thams
61b6(rgyud): cad shes rab thabs bdag nyid// gang mo rdo rje phag mo ni/ gtso bo'i rnam par gnas pa na/ oM b+ho zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i/ sngags kyi'ang yi ge sbyin par bya/ ye shes 'khor lo skye gnas te/ gdan kyang gas
61b7(rgyud): ba phar 'dod// thams cad bde ba'i rnam par 'gyur// bde brtan pa dang 'gro ba dang / bde bkar po bde ba gnag/ bde ba kun tu skyes te bzhin/ bde ba shes rab bde ba thabs// rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba dran// 
61b8(rgyud): rang byung bde ba mi rnams la// rang nyid dkyil 'khor rdzogs ldan du'o// rdzogs ldan rgyud du srung 'di ste// rdzogs ldan nyid ni 'byung ba'o// 'jig rten sna tshogs rdzogs ldan shes// sna tshogs khams rdza gos lnga
62a1(rgyud): de bzhin// sna tshogs 'jig rten khams rnams// de ltar dus kun shes bya// dus cig la ni rdzogs ldan pa sdogs// 'jig rten khams rnams su byung ma ni/ bcom ldan 'das ni gnyis byas pas// 
62a2(rgyud): kun tu bde bas khyad par gcod// gang du rtsod tus der rdzogs ldan/ gang tu rdzogs ldan der rtsod dus// der sum bcu ldan gnyis ldan/ re re yi ni gnyis ldan te/ rnal 'byor rgyud ni sum bcu drug/ ma lus 'dus
62a3(rgyud): las yang 'byung ba'o// dpa' bo thams cad mnyam sbyor bas// rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje 'kha' 'gro de bzhin gshegs// bcom ldan bdag pos 'di gsungs so// zhes bya ba ni dpal 'kha'
62a4(rgyud): 'gro rgya mtsho rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po las// rdo rje sems dpa' dang phag mo'i ga cha skyed pa'i mtshan nyid kyi cho gaste/ le'u bcu bdun pa'o// // de nas slar yang cho ga yi/ srung
62a5(rgyud): kha rnam snang mdzad kyi ste// 'go bor rgyas bdab de ni gsang sngags na ma had nyid do// gyen tu 'gro dus rnal 'byor ni// gang ga bde ba las byung ba'i las// de'i dus su shes bya ste// gus pas mdo/ 
62a6(rgyud): par srung ba'i sngags// bri med 'gron por sbyar bya ste// 'di ni bde chen 'khor lha'o// rnal 'byor bdan tu shes bya ste/ gshin rje ma yis 'khyud de bzhin// oM yaM sngags las skyes bdag nyid/ shes rab tha bra/ 
62a7(rgyud): bdag rgyu yis ni// ya ro mo tsa na na/ de ltar khams gsum rnamasu sbyar bar bya/ lus la sogs pa kun tham pas/ zung dang bzung du 'byung bar 'gyur// de phyir gsuM ba'i yi ga ge ni// gshin rje ma ni 'byung ba/ 
62a8(rgyud): 'gyur// 'pho ba lta bu bde ba'i thabs/ sum ldan rkang bcing las so// snang ba gang tu 'dod pa ni/ rnam par snang 'dzad rang nyid 'gro/ gtso bo'i rnam pa yi ni gzugs/ slar yang sum bcu bdun bdag
62b1(rgyud): tu'o// sngags rnams kyi yid las byung ba las// bral ba'i dbus su shes par bya// sngon du bshad pa'i sngags las 'dir// gang zhig gang gis dbang po yis// 'di'i sngags kun rim pa yasi// 
62b2(rgyud): ni de dang de ye shes bya ba// lhag ma thams cad mnyam pa ste// bsgom pa dang ni bzlas pa mchog/ thams cad yod ma ni med pa 'ang ma ni// ka 'gro thams cad pa man pa'o// sgyu ma yas ni thams cad rmongs// 
62b3(rgyud): mkhas pa sgyu mi nyid kyis grol// phan pa sgyu ma phan ye shes/ sems bskyed pa dang phan pa'o// de ltar na ma hi'i don to// mkhas pa lhag ma bde ba ste/ rnam par snang 'gyur 'bar gyur pas// bde de rnam par
62b4(rgyud): snang 'dzad kyi'o// gshin rje gnon pa'i rig ma ni// gshin rje ma de brjod par 'gyur// gang phyir ba'i srung ba 'di drin pas// dus kun tu ni bya ba bya// snyang kha dpral ba'i ye shes ni/ gnyis med ye
62b5(rgyud): shes mtshan nyid do// rnal 'byor ma rnams don chen phyir/ rgyud rnams kun ni skyed pa'o// rgyud thams cad du gzhan pa'o// rnal 'gyu ra dag byed yod ma yin/ rgyud 'di yi ni rnal 'byor che/ rgyud thams
62b6(rgyud): tu dag byed yin// dkyil 'khor gtso mo gshin rje mas/ de nas slar yang bya ba yang // mngal du bzhugs las bral ba dang / skyed pa dang ni 'pho gnyis kyis/ gshin rje ma dang rnam snang 'dzad/ der ni gzugs dang ga bya
62b7(rgyud): med 'gyur// bde ba'i sdug bsngal can ye shes// lha rdzas phyag rgyas ro mnyam bya/ dpa' bo thams cad mnyam sbyor las// rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje 'khra' 'gro de bzhin gshegs// bcom ldan pad
62b8(rgyud): pos 'di gsungs so// dpal 'kha' 'gro rgya mtsho rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po las// rnam par snang 'dzad la sogs pa'i cho ga ste/ le'u bco brgyad pa'o// // de nas pad ma gar gi dbang / go cha'i srung
63a1(rgyud): ba bka' bstsal pa// 'dod chags me ni gsal bzhin pa// spyi bor 'gro ba stobs chen te// sa twa hU~M gi sngags yi ga dang / hri maM mongs pa'i sgyu ma yis/ shes rab thabs kyi rang bzhin ni// nam
63a2(rgyud): mkha'i 'khor lo'i gtso bo'o// kha'i pad ma rmongs byed ma'ang // ro dang ro min can srung ba// lce dang lce ni 'dus pa la/ thig le mya ngan rnal 'byor pas pa/ mchog tu dga' ba skyes pa ni// ye shes can med ye shes
63a3(rgyud): ldan pa'ang med// me dang me mo la bstan pas/ 'dul ba zhes bya rang sems so/ dga' ba'i ngag gi tshogs rnams ni// chos sgrogs pa yis rgyud yin no// byang chub sems kyi bu ga ni/ de ru dbyugs ni rgyu ba'o// 
63a4(rgyud): bu ga rnam pa tshogs bshad// de rnams su dbyugs mngon rgyus so/ bu ga kun tu hri sbyin bya// mi 'gyur mchog zhi ba'o// ma~M yang zhing sde 'go la/ mi 'gyur mchog las 'du ba'o// rmongs pa yis ni srad
63a5(rgyud): sbyor ba/ yang dag lam tu rab 'jug byed// des na rmongs pa lar grags to// srid pa'i 'khor lo 'joms ma'o// srid pa med pa mchog kyang med// de ni kha sbyor du brjod do// bsngags de nyid
63a6(rgyud): kyi sbyor ba yis/ dkyil 'khor gsum bcu bdun bdag nyid/ gtso bo dpa' ba 'am lha mo ste/ spyi myug dang ni kha'i dbus su// thams cad du ni srung byed dang / rtog pa thams cad bajoms byed pa'o// pad mngon na
63a7(rgyud): pa'i ye shes// sangs rgyas rnams kyi byang chub gzugs// kun rdzob shes byed shes bya ni/ gar dbang phyung tu rjod pa nyid// byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzugs/ byang chub rang gi thams cad rtogs/

63b1(rgyud): bzhin med dang bde bdag nyid/ de ni kha sbyor du rjod do// dpa' bo thams cad mnyam sbyor bas// rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje 'kha' 'gro de bzhin gshegs// bcom ldan bdag pos 'di gsungs//

63b3(rgyud): he ru ka'i srung ba/ go cha slar yang bshad par bya/ 'gren dang dpung por yong ba ste/ rnal 'byor ma'i 'go bor ro// b+ho Sha Ta ye sngags mnyam pa// 'byung dang 'byung dang byung ba srung // hriM hrIM tu skyod pa'i sngags/ de phyir
63b4(rgyud): shes rab thabs bdag nyid// he ni sems bdag nyid rnal 'byor// slar yang ru ni dag bdag nyid// ka lus kyi rang bzhin nyid rnal 'byor// sa 'og sa steng mtho 'jig rten/ bde ba'i thog mtha' dbus
63b5(rgyud): su ni/ b+h+yo Sha Ta he sa bon can// hri hr-i 'og dang steng shes bya// srog gi/ rlung gis skyod pa yis// gtong dang dga' ba la goms dang // hU~Mpa can gyi sbyor ba'i dus/ de'i dus su 'khor lo ni/ sum bdun bdun
63b6(rgyud): bdag nyid shes bya/ de ltar dus ni bzhi rnams kyi// ji lta'i rim par de 'dod de/ sngags de nyid kyi rnal 'byor gyis/ mchod pa mchog tu rmad bu byung / de ltar rnam shes brgyad rnams kyi/ gcig dang gnyis dang gsum
63b7(rgyud): dang ldan// le'u bzhi'i rnal 'byor gyis// ji lta'i rim pas rtogs pa'o// spyod pa'i rgyud ni gsum pa la// le'u ru ni 'byung ba dang / bya ba le'u bzhi pa ru/ rgyud ni rang bzhin bskyed pa dbang // de kho na nyid bdan skyes pa/ 
63b8(rgyud): slar yang gsum par brjod pa ya ni// bzhi pa ru ni gzhan gyi bdan/ skyes pa ye shes pha rol 'gro// bsrung ba 'gro ba bzhin rnams kyis/ lha dang mi dang 'dre dang ni/ klu'i 'gro bar mkhas pa yan/ shes bya kun tu rgyu
64a1(rgyud): rnams kyi'o// de de'i rang bzhin dus rnams ni// bskal pa bzang por chud pa yis// de bzhin gshegs pa 'drongs mi 'gyur// slar yang 'gro med skye mi 'gyur/ rang bzhin shes par gyur nas ni// sems can
64a2(rgyud): gang gis rang bzhin 'gyur// lta bu bdun bcu gnyis rnams ni// kun tu skyod pa'i las kyis so// nyan thos rnams kyi ltas pa lda// rang sangs rgyas kyi lta ba gnyis// rnal 'byor spyod pa yi ni bdun// dbu ma mchog rnams
64a3(rgyud): kyi ni rgyad/ bcu drug pha rol phyin rnams kyi/ gsang sngags theg pa'i sum bcu drug/ bdun dang rgyang pa'i gnyis kyis mnan// kun kyang sngags kyi theg pa'o// rtsa ba'i kun kyang sngags kyi theg pa'o// rtsa'i kun sbyor rtsa ba
64a4(rgyud): can// bla ma'i drin las shes par bya// he ru ka ma rtsa ba 'dzad/ srid dang myang ngan 'das dbus bzhugs/ dpa' bo thams cad mnyam basbyor bas// rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje 'kha'agro de bzhi
64a5(rgyud): gshegs// bcom ldan bdag pos 'di gsungs so// zhes/ bya ba ni dpal mkha' 'gro rgya 'tsho rnal 'byor me'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po las/ he ru ka la sogs pa'i srung ba'i go cha'i cho ga'i le'u
64a6(rgyud): sde/ nyi shu pa'o// // de nas rdo rje nyi ma yi// bsrung ba'i bshad par bya ba ni/ hUM hU~M ho'i sngags 'di yis/ mig gi dbang po'i dbus su ni// hUM yig gnyis kyi sbyor ba yis/ lta ba thams cad 'thong bar gyur/ 
64a7(rgyud): ye shes rnam shes mchi ma yis/ 'og dang steng du thim pa las// lta ba bdun bcu rtsa gnyis ni// dus gcig tu ni mthong bar 'gyur/ 'grin pa'i bu ga ru ni lnga/ gsang ba'i rdo rje can tu gnyis// bdun ni snying khar
64a8(rgyud): yang dag gshad/ brgyad ni glang ba'i rgyas su'o// bcu drug gtsug tor du ni 'gyur/ lte dkyil 'khor du sum bcu drug/ ma lus rang gi las kyis skyed/ rang gi lta ba 'dir mthong 'gyur/ 'di de bdag gi gdan
64b1(rgyud): te// sa gsum lta bur mthong ba yin// ho yig sems dpa' ma kun gyi/ mtha' mayas pa'i sangs rgyas zhing / rdo rje nyi mas khyab par 'gyur// de phyir mig ni bsrung bar byed/ kun tu skrag byed mas 'khyud pa// hU~M hU~M gsang
64b2(rgyud): sngags sgra sgrogs ma/ skrag pa'i yi ge gnyis kyis ni/ sdig pa thams cad mthar byed pa'o// sum bcu bdun bdag dkyil 'khor gyi// dbus su gnyis ni bsgom par bya// sngon gsungs sngags kyi gzugs kyis
64b3(rgyud): ni// lha rnams kun du 'byung bar 'gyur/ re re yis ni lta ba yis// de la bsrung ba byed par 'gyur/ rnal 'byor ma yis nam mkha' gang / slar yang ldan skyes rdzogs byang chub// rnal 'byor ma ni lhan skyes gzugs// lha na
64b4(rgyud): skyes yi ge rnal 'byor ma// rnal 'byor ma yis lhan skyes zos// slar yang rnal 'byor ma za 'gyur/ sangs rgyas gzugs ni rnal 'byor ma/ rdo rje 'dzin ma'i gzugs can ma/ gnas kyi gzugs
64b5(rgyud): ni nal 'byor ma/ byas dang byeda'ang de bzhin no// sgrub bya mdzang sa kyi bster bar 'gyur/ go cha'i yige sgom pa la'o// sgrub pa ci dang ci 'dod pa/ de rnams kyi ni rnal 'byor ma/ tshul 'di sgom pa med pa
64b6(rgyud): ma yi/ sems can de rnams rmongs par 'gyur/ yi ga bkod pa tsam gyis ni/ las rgyal thams cad byed par 'gyur/ dpa'o thams cad mnyam sbyor las// rdo rje sems dpa' bde bas mchog/ rdo rje la
64b7(rgyud): 'gro de bzhin gshegs// bcom ldan bdag pos 'di gsungs so// zhes bya ba ni dpal 'kha' 'gro rgya mtsho rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po las// rdo rje nyi ma la spogs pa'i go cha'i bsrung ba'i rtsa
64b8(rgyud): ga'i le'u ste/ nyi shu rtsa gcig pa'o// de nas rta mchog go bsrung ba/ thams cad bya ba byed dge'o// phaT haM sngags kyi rnal 'byor gyis// kun nas 'go dang rkang pa'i mthar/ mdzod su
66a1(rgyud): dbus su dgod bya ste// spyi gtsug dbus su rnal 'byor ma// 'gon por kun skrag ma shes nas/ tshags kun dang ni na mkha' zhes/ gtum po'i gsang sngags paT phaT ste// ye shes

66b1(rgyud): de bzhin// 'gro dang 'ong dang gnyis gnyis te// go cha bcu gnyis der de bzhin// dpa' bo yul kyi mtshan nyid kyis// dngos po'i mtshan nyid der gar byed// rnal 'byor ba dang rtsi nyid 'byung 'gyur// zang za khams
66b2(rgyud): rnams za bar ste// steng dang 'og tu mtshon ltas pas// lhan skyes bdag nyid rtsen par byed// rjes ldan drug gi sbyor ba yis// sgrub pa po yis byas pa yan/ dbang po thams cad mnyam sbyor bas// rdo rje sems /

66b4(rgyud): pa'i go cha'i bsrung ba ste/ cho ga'i le'u ste nyi shu rtsa gnyis/ 'o// // de nas tor ma'i de nyid bshad/ mthar kyis ji dalta ba bzhin no// chos 'byung dbus su son pa ni/ ji lta'i cho ga
66b5(rgyud): gtor ma sbyin/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug 'kha' 'gro'i gzugs/ slar yang go cha sogs pas bsrung / de'i ting 'dzin dmigs par bya// pad ma'i snod ni gzhag bya ste/ phyi dang nang bdag nyid du bya/ 
66b6(rgyud): a ba d+hu tiri skye gnas brig lte ba'i 'og dang steng bu ga/ pad ma'i snod du rtag par bya// na mkha' lnga'i btud rtsi ni/ thams cad ro snyam par bya'o// phung po ko ku da ha na sogs// skye 'tshed rnams ni
66b7(rgyud): sha kun te// sbar ba bde ba'i sems kyis ni/ 'dod chags me'i sa sro'o// sbyang ba mchog ni bdag nyid la'o// slar yang btud rtsir byed pa ste// bsam gtan phyag rgyun du der/ sku gsum du ni byin
66b8(rgyud): kyis rlabasaka sngags dang phyag rgya'i bsgyur ba yasi/ mkha' 'gro ma rnams spyan drangs bya/ rtse mo mdung byas nges par ni// gung mo rtse bya 'theb rdo rje/ rten pa yang dag rtsir byas nas/ dpal ba'i phyogs

300a1(rgyud): kyib mi khya 'i/ 'a rten pa ros thams cad dag pa'i ma jug pas/ 'o ma'i lung bstan no// gtsigs par la skyom pa dag dar srus te/ rab tu bsngags pa'i ses 'thos// 'dzin 'a chen pam/

300a4(rgyud): ma/ rAdz+dza/ 8/ bsngags kyi rgyal po brjod pa tsam gyis/ sdig pa thams cad nges par zad par byed par 'gyur ro// thams cad 'di sna tshogs su 'phrul ba tsam brtsams par bya'o// dpas
